<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">trôosten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">trōsten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*traustijaną</i>. </p>

***troostprijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:troostprijs.html>troostprijs</a> (31517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troost.html>troost</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">consolation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prize, reward</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troostprijs.html>troostprijs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troostprijzen.html>troostprijzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troostprijs.html>troostprijsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>consolation prize, a prize awarded to a runner-up or other well performing non-winning participants.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tropisch.html>tropisch</a></i> (from Latin) or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tropicus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τροπικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tropikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The senses relating to the tropics certainly derive from German.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tropisch.html>tropisch</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tropisch.html>tropischer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tropisch.html>tropisch</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tropical <span class="defdate">[from early 19th c.]</span></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pertaining to the rotations of a celestial body, especially in relation to the tropical year <span class="defdate">[17th <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 18th or 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> metaphorical, figurative <span class="defdate">[17th <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 19th c.]</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tros.html>tros</a> (44490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tors.html>tors</a></i> with metathesis. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. <hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>raceme</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of fruit</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> cluster, bunch, string (of berries)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">trosse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">trousse</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>hawser</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tros.html>tros</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trots.html>trots</a> (719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Early modern borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Trotz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">defiance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">traz</i>, of unknown origin.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>pride

***trousseau.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a> (98477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">trousse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bundle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">trousseaus</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">trousseaux</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> and linen, etc., that a bride collects for her wedding and married life.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1906</b> September 29,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Literary_Digest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Literary Digest">The Literary Digest</a></cite>, volume XXXIII, number 13 (whole no., 858), New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Funk_%26_Wagnalls" class="extiw" title="w:Funk amp; Wagnalls">Funk amp; Wagnalls Company</a>, publishers, 44 to 60 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/23rd_Street_(Manhattan)" class="extiw" title="w:23rd Street (Manhattan)">East 23d Steet</a>, New York, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/17880968">17880968</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=03JFAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA439">page 439</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>Trousseaus</b> of German Heiresses.—Despatches from Berlin <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> recently of the visit to that city of a wealthy German mother and her two daughters. for the purpose of buying <b>trousseaus</b> for the <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a> who are <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to be perhaps the richest heiresses of the world. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:frau.html>Frau</a> Krupp, widow of the great gunmaker of <a href = vnd.unilang:essen.html>Essen</a>  | <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Friedrich_Alfred_Krupp" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Friedrich Alfred Krupp">Friedrich Alfred Krupp</a> | , and her daughters, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bertha_Krupp" class="extiw" title="w:Bertha Krupp"><a href = vnd.unilang:bertha.html>Bertha</a></a> and Barbara, have just <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> here, the object of their visit being to buy the wedding-<b>trousseaus</b> for her daughters.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1918</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leo_Tolstoy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Leo Tolstoy"><a href = vnd.unilang:leo.html>Leo</a> Tolstoy</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aylmer_and_Louise_Maude" class="extiw" title="w:Aylmer and Louise Maude"><a href = vnd.unilang:louise.html>Louise</a> and Aylmer Maude</a>, transl., <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anna_Karenina" class="extiw" title="w:Anna Karenina"><a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a> Karenina, a Novel</a></i> (World's Classics; 211), [Cambridge?]: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oxford_University_Press" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oxford University Press">Oxford University Press</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/oclc/6561729">6561729</a></small>; republished Oxford: Oxford University Press, 1998, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> 978-0-19-158623-1</small>, page 435:
<dl><dd>Consequently, having decided to divide her daughter's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></b> into two parts, a lesser and a larger, the Princess eventually consented to have the wedding before <a href = vnd.unilang:advent.html>Advent</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Denyse Baillargeon |  Yvonne <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>Klein</a>, transl.,  <cite>Making Do: Women, Family and Home in Montreal during the Great Depression</cite> (Studies in Childhood and Family in Canada), Waterloo, <a href = vnd.unilang:ont.html>Ont</a>. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wilfrid_Laurier_University_Press" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wilfrid Laurier University Press">Wilfrid <a href = vnd.unilang:laurier.html>Laurier</a> University Press</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 60:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In a study of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></b> in France, Agnès Fine observes that, regardless of its contents and its value, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></b> represented an essential in women's <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a>; through the first <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of the twentieth century, at least, it seemed altogether inconceivable to be married without the provision of a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></b>. But while in the sixteenth century it involved the furniture of a bride's bedroom, bit by bit the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trousseau.html>trousseau</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reduced to linen, especially to sheets.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Paul <a href = vnd.unilang:sant.html>Sant</a> Cassia |  Constantina <a href = vnd.unilang:bada.html>Bada</a>,  <cite>The Making of the Modern Greek Family: Marriage and Exchange in Nineteenth-century Athens</cite> (Cambridge Studies in Social and Cultural Anthropology), Cambridge |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cambridge_University_Press" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cambridge University Press">Cambridge University Press</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 81:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> further significance in the transmission of cash and <b>trousseaux</b>. To begin with, they appear in inverse proportion to each other across time, for example <b>trousseaux</b> appear more important in the eighteenth century, whereas by the 1830s they <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> declined in favour of cash endowments.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bundle.</li></ol>
</body>

***trouw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trouw.html>trouw</a> (1306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouwe.html>trouwe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">triuwa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trewwō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouw.html>trouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouwen.html>trouwen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouw.html>trouwtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>loyalty, faithfulness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>Groot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>Uw</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trouw.html>trouw</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>Heer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Great <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Thy <i>faithfulness</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a> Lord.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>marriage</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouwe.html>trouwe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*triuwi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*triwwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>true, faithful, loyal</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouwen.html>trouwen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*triuwon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trewwāną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trouw.html>trouw</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:truffel.html>truffel</a> (52985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">truffe</i>, which ultimately derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tuber</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:truffel.html>truffel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:truffel.html>truffels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:truffel.html>truffeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a truffle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a magic truffle, the sclerotia of magic mushrooms</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tsaar.html>tsaar</a> (16023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">царь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">цьсарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cĭsarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*cěsařь</i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaisaraz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:caesar.html>Caesar</a></i>.
</p>

</p>

***tuba.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a> (20932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tube, trumpet, military trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, first borrowed as a historic term in the 18th century. The name of the modern instrument <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed in the 19th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>Tuba</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Baß-Tuba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bass <a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the same Latin source.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tubas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A large brass musical instrument, usually in the bass range, played through a vibration of the <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a> upon the mouthpiece and fingering of the keys.
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, Thomas D. Rossing, <i>The Science of Sound‎</i>, page 230
<dl><dd>One version of the large <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></b>, popular in <a href = vnd.unilang:marching.html>marching</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bands.html>bands</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called a sousaphone in honor of bandsman John Philip Sousa.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A type of Roman military trumpet, distinct from the modern <a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a>.</li>
<li>A large <a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:organs.html>organs</a>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">grunt-horn</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A Malayan plant whose roots are a significant source of <a href = vnd.unilang:rotenone.html>rotenone</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Derris_malaccensis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Derris malaccensis"><i>Derris malaccensis</i></a></span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cebuano_language" class="extiw" title="w:Cebuano language">Cebuano</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ceb"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tubas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A reddish <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/palm_wine" class="extiw" title="w:palm wine">palm wine</a> made from coconut or nipa <a href = vnd.unilang:sap.html>sap</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tubas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tubae</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tube or tubular organ.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tuba.html>tuba</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziekinstrument.html>muziekinstrument</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koperen.html>koperen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blaasinstrument.html>blaasinstrument</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lage.html>lage</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tucht.html>tucht</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tuht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tuhtiz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuchthuis.html>tuchthuis</a> (38804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tucht.html>tucht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">discipline</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A house of correction, closed penitentiary where 'wayward' inmates (especially youth and vagrants) are to be punished and (at least initially) reeducated trough forced labor, under threat of beatings</li>

***tuig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuig.html>tuig</a> (3388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tuyg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tools, apparatus, utensil, ornament</span><span title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tiug</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tiugiją</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*teugą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stuff, matter, device</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*teuhaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lead, bring, pull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dewk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pull, lead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeug.html>Zeug</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing, device</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***tuigen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuigen.html>tuigen</a> (30210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuig.html>tuig</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuigen.html>tuigen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rig (a sailing ship)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to harness, to put a harness on</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tugen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tiugon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***tuimelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuimelaar.html>tuimelaar</a> (58878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tumelaer</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuimelen.html>tuimelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuimelaar.html>tuimelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuimelaars.html>tuimelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuimelaar.html>tuimelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who tumbles.</li>
<li>A common bottlenose dolphin, <i>Tursiops truncatus</i>.</li>
<li>A rocker <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">implement or machine working with a <a href = vnd.unilang:rocking.html>rocking</a> motion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:tumbler.html>tumbler</a> pigeon <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">domesticated pigeon, variety of <i>Columba <a href = vnd.unilang:livia.html>livia</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tuimelaar.html>tuimelaar</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tuun</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tūn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tūną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*dūnom</i>.

***tuinbouw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuinbouw.html>tuinbouw</a> (72320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuin.html>tuin</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuinbouw.html>tuinbouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The agricultural cultivation of non-grass (non-grain) crops including certain food crops and ornamental plants and flowers, especially by means of specialised equipment such as greenhouses; also the branch of agriculture in which these crops are cultivated.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In Dutch, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tuinbouw.html>tuinbouw</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often perceived as being distinct from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:landbouw.html>landbouw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">agriculture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which includes <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:akkerbouw.html>akkerbouw</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veeteelt.html>veeteelt</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tuinbouw.html>tuinbouw</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuinbouw.html>tuinbouw</a></a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:landbouw.html>landbouw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:specifiek.html>specifiek</a> toelegt <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:intensief.html>intensief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijze.html>wijze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:telen.html>telen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groenten.html>groenten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bloemen.html>bloemen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bomen.html>bomen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bollen.html>bollen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:zaden.html>zaden</a>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tute</i>. ***tulband.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tulband.html>tulband</a> (25997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">tülbent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">دلبند</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dülbend</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">دلبند</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolband</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The second element <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> adapted to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></i> by folk etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tulband.html>tulband</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tulbanden.html>tulbanden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tulband.html>tulbandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">turban</span>.</li>
<li>A cake baked in the shape of a turban.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">tulipe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">tülbent</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fine muslin, turban</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">دلبند</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolband</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turban</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***tumbleweed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tumbleweed.html>tumbleweed</a> (30858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tumble</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">weed</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tumbleweed.html>tumbleweed</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tumbleweeds</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any plant which habitually <a href = vnd.unilang:breaks.html>breaks</a> away from its roots in the autumn, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> driven by the wind, as a light, rolling mass, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the fields and <a href = vnd.unilang:prairies.html>prairies</a>; as witch grass, wild indigo, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Amaranthus_albus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Amaranthus albus"><i>Amaranthus <a href = vnd.unilang:albus.html>albus</a></i></a></span>, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">attributive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Describing unwanted silence and inactivity. Often used of a situation when one <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a statement that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ignored or ill-received by one's audience, as the resultant silence <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> likened to that of a desolate desert with rolling tumbleweeds.</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b> January 21,  “Plsntgrn”, in  <cite>alt.music.progressive</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://groups.google.com/group/rec.music.progressive/msg/c5bc2926d0712699">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Putting an ad in the local paper that Spock's Beard and Arena are in town will get you a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tumbleweed.html>tumbleweed</a></b> response and some wasted revenue.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:trevor.html>Trevor</a> Wright,  <cite>How to Be a Brilliant English Teacher</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=5V64WA533MoC">[2]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 68:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“Why do <a href = vnd.unilang:families.html>families</a> argue?” may only induce the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tumbleweed.html>tumbleweed</a></b> response. (Could you answer that question out of the blue?)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A tan colour, like that of a <a href = vnd.unilang:tumbleweed.html>tumbleweed</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:tumbleweed.html>tumbleweed</a> colour: <span style="background-color:DEA681; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>
